MODULE 4:
Topic: pipeline
```verilog
module clock_gate_D_ff_en_W32_0_6 (CLK, EN, TE, ENCLK);
  input CLK, EN, TE;
  output ENCLK;

  reg [1:0] stage1, stage2;

  always @(posedge CLK) begin
    if (EN) begin
      stage1 <= TE ? 1'b1 : 1'b0;
      stage2 <= stage1;
    end
  end

  assign ENCLK = stage2 & CLK;

endmodule
```

MODULE 5:
Topic: pipeline
```verilog
module shift_register ( input clk, input d, output q );

  reg [2:0] register;
  wire [2:0] next_register;

  assign next_register = {register[1:0], d};

  always @(posedge clk) begin
    register <= next_register;
  end

  assign q = register[2];

endmodule
```
